local Vh=(function(as,ru)
    as=_i(as)
    local cd=xh()
    local function Nc(Xl,Uu)
        local Qm=(function(...)
            return{...},il('#',...)
        end)
        local vt;
        vt=(function(nd,Dh,g)
            if Dh>g then
                return
            end
            return nd[Dh],vt(nd,Dh+1,g)
        end)
        local function z(do_,xi,ye,R)
            local mm,zo,De,vl,Tm,du,_f,rp,fb,Xe,wb,_g,Ga,qq,Am,Ic,pm,pu,Pb,ak,Sm,zu,mr,nm;

            end,{};
